Let's work with that let crazy = 0; const crazy_ans = [3414, 3311, 3442, 3385, 2006, 2108, 2110, 2112, 2117]; // CYOA helper functions :: Making TCT Beautiful Again // Returns the index for a specific question pk // Recall; arrays start at 0 check_q = function(q_pk) { // Very compact function // Finds index where pk equals given; returns value // -1 : means question not found return campaignTrail_temp.questions_json.findIndex( function (i){ return i.pk == q_pk; } ); } // Swaps an answer in a given question swap_ans = function(old_pk, new_pk) { // Finds indices of both answers via PK let o = campaignTrail_temp.answers_json.findIndex(function (i){return i.pk == old_pk}); let n = campaignTrail_temp.answers_json.findIndex(function (i){return i.pk == new_pk}); // Error handling; // result as -1 --> answer not found if (o == -1) { console.log(`⚠️ answer with PK ${old_pk} not found!!`); return; } if (n == -1) { console.log(`⚠️ answer with PK ${new_pk} not found!!`); return; } // Swaps the questions for the respective answers [campaignTrail_temp.answers_json[o].fields.question, campaignTrail_temp.answers_json[n].fields.question] = [campaignTrail_temp.answers_json[n].fields.question, campaignTrail_temp.answers_json[o].fields.question]; return; } // Drops in a specific question at a specified index :: lossy method // Recall; arrays start at 0 swap_in_one = function(num, new_pk, new_desc) { // Swaps in the new question... // Get the PK and description right! else you will encounter bugs campaignTrail_temp.questions_json[num].pk = new_pk; campaignTrail_temp.questions_json[num].fields.description = new_desc; return; } // Ever wonder what happens when you answer a question while CYOA is on? if (imgg != null) { imgg.src = sr; } } // Pageflip functions pg_forward = function(curr) { document.getElementById(`screen${curr}`).style.display = "none"; document.getElementById(`screen${curr + 1}`).style.display = "initial"; document.getElementById(`screen0`).style.display = "initial"; } // Faithless elector function // Called depending on conditions in endings function // All inputs are state or candidate IDs except vote count faithless = function(state, cid = campaignTrail_temp.candidate_id, cid_guard = -1, votes = true){ // Gets the electoral vote count const state_obj = campaignTrail_temp.states_json[campaignTrail_temp.states_json.findIndex(function (i){return i.pk == state})]; const ev_count = state_obj.fields.electoral_votes; // Gets the index of state election results const i_r = campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results.findIndex(function (i){return i.state == state}); let state_res = campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results[i_r]["result"]; // Won't reallocate any electors if said candidate already won the state if (state_res[0]["candidate"] == cid) { return; } // The cid_guard variable makes sure a certain candidate (not the 1st one) MUST win a state for the faithless electors to confer // If this isn't the case the rest of the function won't kick in if (state_res[0]["candidate"] != cid_guard && cid_guard != -1) { return; } // Clear existing electoral votes campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results[i_r]["result"].forEach((num, i, arr) => { arr[i].electoral_votes = 0; }); // Default conditions; gives you every electoral vote // :: wait...what's this, greater than?? // :: just another guard condition :) if (votes === true || votes >= ev_count){ campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results[i_r]["result"][state_res.findIndex(function (i){return i.candidate == cid})]["electoral_votes"] = ev_count; } else { // Otherwise it just transfers a certain number of electoral votes campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results[i_r]["result"][0]["electoral_votes"] = (ev_count - votes); campaignTrail_temp.final_state_results[i_r]["result"][state_res.findIndex(function (i){return i.candidate == cid})]["electoral_votes"] = votes; } // Does its work on the overall results to reflect changes ev_delta = (votes === true || votes >= ev_count) ? ev_count : votes; campaignTrail_temp.final_overall_results[campaignTrail_temp.final_overall_results.findIndex(function (i){return i.candidate == cid})]["electoral_votes"] += ev_delta; campaignTrail_temp.final_overall_results[campaignTrail_temp.final_overall_results.findIndex(function (i){return i.candidate == state_res[0]["candidate"]})]["electoral_votes"] -= ev_delta; return; } // Endings (most of this is self explanatory) campaignTrail_temp.multiple_endings = true; It seemed like the people weren't going to just choose from the political establishment anymore, that they were going to try something new -- at least a few of them were, enough to make a difference.

Then nothing happened. They held their noses, like they always did, and voted for the status quo. Dennis made no difference. The Democrats' hold on power would continue, uninterested in the real needs of Americans.

\"It doesn't matter now,\" Dennis said to himself, glancing down at the speech in his hands. He felt his cellphone in his pocket. No one was going to call him.

The only people who cared were here, in The Land.
